# Text Elements
Lenz said about polarity by saying that
if they made a loop the current will be in such a direction
that Bind by Iind in such a way that Bind opposes
Borginal that produced the Iind in the first
place ^pDVApC5S

BI should be opposite of Bo based on current
direction we can get emf polarity ^s5nrCSMK
